

<h3>MAIN CONFERENCE</h3>

  <h3 id="awards">CVPR 2019 Awards</h3>
  
  <ul>

  <li><p><b>Best Paper Award</b></p></li>
    <ul>
      <li><p>"A Theory of Fermat Paths for Non-Line-of-Sight Shape Reconstruction" by Shumian Xin, Sotiris Nousias, Kyros Kutulakos, Aswin Sankaranarayanan, Srinivasa G. Narasimhan and Ioannis Gkioulekas.</p></li>
    </ul>
  <li><p><b>Best Student Paper Award</b></p></li>
    <ul>
      <li><p>"Reinforced Cross-Modal Matching and Self-Supervised Imitation Learning for Vision-Language Navigation" by Xin Wang, Qiuyuan Huang, Asli Celikyilmaz, Jianfeng Gao, Dinghan Shen, Yuan-Fang Wang, William Yang Wang and Lei Zhang.</p></li>
    </ul>
  <li><p><b>Best Paper Honorable Mention</b></p></li>
  <ul>
    <li><p>"A Style-Based Generator Architecture for Generative Adversarial Networks" by Tero Karras, Samuli Laine and Timo Aila.</p></li>
    <li><p>"Learning the Depths of Moving People by Watching Frozen People" by Zhengqi Li, Tali Dekel, Forrester Cole, Richard Tucker, Ce Liu, Bill Freeman and Noah Snavely.</p></li>
  </ul>
  <li><p><b>PAMI Longuet-Higgins Prize (Retrospective Most Impactful Paper from CVPR 2009)</b></p></li>
    <ul>
      <li><p>"ImageNet: A large-scale hierarchical image database" by Jia Deng, Wei Dong, Richard Socher, Li-Jia Li, Kai Li, and Li Fei-Fei.</p></li>
    </ul>
  <li><p><b>PAMI Young Researcher Award</b></p></li>
    <ul>
      <li><p>Karen Simonyan</p></li>
    </ul>
  <li><p><b>2019 Computer Pioneer Award</b></p></li>
    <ul>
      <li><p>Jitendra Malik</p></li>
    </ul>
  </ul>
